48.16(1): sam/ bdag ni nam yang ma rig 'khrul pa'i blos/ lus ngag yid gsum spyod lam 
48.17(1): shin du rtsing / bder gshegs rgyal ba rnams kyi thugs ma mnyes/ mkhyen ldan drung 
48.18(1): du dus 'dir bshags par 'bul/ bdag ni khyed la mos 'dun 'di ltar che/ nyid

48.21(1): las 'phro dang / da lta'i gnas skabs bsod nams 'brel ba yis/ bder gshegs

49.18(1): bshags/ 'byor ldan phun sum tshogs pa'i dngos grub stsol/ bdag ni dal 'byor

49.22(1): bder gshegs rgyal ba rnams la mthol lo bshags/
50.1(1): ltar ma bsgrub pas/ mkhas dang grub pa'i gshen la mthol lo bshags/ brgyad khri 
50.2(1): bzhi stong rtogs grol dngos grub stsol/ bdag ni g.yung drung bon la spyod pa'i dus/
50.3(1): bka' ltar ma bgyis lung ltar ma bsgrub pas/ lung rgyud 'dren pa'i gshen la 
50.4(1): mthol lo bshags/ bon spyod tshul dang ldan pa'i dngos grub gsol/ bdag ni phyi 
50.5(1): rgyud bon la spyod pa'i dus/ ma mthong rdzun dang log pa'i lung ston byas/ gto rgyud 
50.6(1): 'bum sde'i gshen la mthol lo bshags/ 'bum sde sil bur mkhyen pa'i dngos grub 
50.7(1): gsol/ bdag ni dpyad rgyud bon la spyod pa'i dus/ mkhas par ma bslab lag 
50.8(1): len tshod mda' 'phang / dpyad rgyud khri sde'i gshen la mthol lo bshags/ nyon

50.17(1): 'grogs pa'i dus/ brtse gdung sems kyis sdong grogs ma bgyis pa/ lha sras lcam

51.1(1): bo'i gzhung ltar ma drang bas/ stag la me 'bar sku la mthol lo bshags/ mthu

51.18(1): thabs shes 'du 'bral med pa'i dngos grub stsol/ pho rnams ye nas thabs kyi rang 
51.19(1): bzhin la/ chags sdang ru tra gshe skur btab pa rnams/ sems dpa' rig 'dzin

57.21(1): rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa la/ phyag 'tshal sdig bshags yid rang mchod par 
58.1(1): 'bul/ de dag thams cad yongs su mnyes par shog /tshe rabs sngon nas bsags 
58.2(1): pa'i las 'phro dang / rgyal ba mchod pas mnyes pa'i byin rlabs dang / rgyun rkyen rten 
58.3(1): 'brel 'tshogs pa'i nus mthu yis/ bdag ni myur du sangs rgyas thob par shog /da 
58.4(1): lta 'dir skyes 'jig rten 'di ru yang / tshe ring nad med bsod nams 'phel ba 
58.5(1): dang / bon dang mthun pa'i longs spyod phun sum 'tshogs/ rtag tu bde legs 
58.6(1): bkra shis thob par shog /'dir yang bsam pa'i don rnams yongs su grub/ sgo 
58.7(1): gsum dge ba'i las spyod thams cad kun/ bar chod med par mthar phyin don 
58.8(1): grub nas/ mi lus thob pa don dang ldan par shog /phyi mar bon nyid 'od gsal 
58.9(1): bar do ru/ sgra 'od zer gsum cho 'phrul rtsal du shar/ bon nyid ma bu dbyer med 
58.10(1): rtsal mnyam nas/ sku gsum rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thob par shog /gal te las kyi 
58.11(1): 'khor bar skyes nas kyang / ngan song gsum dang mtha' 'khob gnas spangs nas/
58.12(1): gnas mchog dam pa 'ol mo lung ring dang / sangs rgyas bzhugs pa'i zhing du skye 
58.13(1): bar shog /rigs ngan dman dang za ma mo lus dang / khas zhan dbang chung zha grum 
58.14(1): skyon can sogs/ yid du mi 'ong mi sdug ma yin par/ rigs bzang khung btsun 
58.15(1): lus su skye bar shog /chags tshad ma ldan mgo lus ma 'dzom dang / srin po'i 
58.16(1): gzugs dang mtshan ngan ma yin par/ ngo mtshar dbyibs legs ring thung tshad 
58.17(1): snyoms pa'i/ mdzes pa'i lha bran bzhed pa'i lus thob shog /kha dog nag dang sngo skya 
58.18(1): thal mdog dang / dmar nag bdud zug dud kha ma yin par/ dkar dmar 
58.19(1): mdzes pa me tog tshom bu ris/ ma chags pad ma lta bu'i mdangs thob shog /mi snyan 
58.20(1): skad dang mya ngan u dug sgra/ dig lkugs bar chod 'gag 'dzer ma yin par/
58.21(1): tshangs pa'i skad dang mya ngan sangs pa'i sgra/ gsung snyan khu byug lta bu'i dbyangs 
59.1(1): ldan shog /blo rmongs 'thib dang mi shes rmongs pa can/ ma rig gti mug blun po ma 
59.2(1): yin par/ rang rig ye shes rang grol mngon gyur cing / bon rnams ma bslabs 
59.3(1): thams cad shes par shog /chung nas dad pa'i sems dang rab ldan te/ bla ma dge 
59.4(1): 'dun 'phags pa'i tshogs rnams kyi/ sku rnams mthong nas mos shing dad pa dang /
59.5(1): slar yang zhal mjal thugs rjes zin par shog /las ngan log pa'i phyogs su mi 
59.6(1): sems shing / dkar po'i phyogs la bsam pa rtse gcig pas/ dge ba'i las la rab 
59.7(1): tu 'dun pa'i sems/ skad cig tsam yang 'bral med skye bar shog /'jig rten 
59.8(1): khams kyi don mdzad mang lags kyang / kun gyi nang nas khyad par 'phags gyur pa/
59.9(1): sman gyi gtso bo rnam par rgyal ba bzhin/ rgyal sras dam pa gcig dang mjal bar 
59.10(1): shog /so so skye bo tha ma ma yin par/ chung nas 'dul khrims rnam dag sgor zhugs te/
59.11(1): nyes ltung nyams pa'i dri mas ma gos shing / nyis brgya lnga bcu'i khrims dang ldan par 
59.12(1): shog /bdag ni g.yung drung bon gyi sgor zhugs te/ sgo gsum thang chod le lo med pa 
59.13(1): yis/ brtson 'grus chen po myur ba rab ldan nas/ bon sgo gang spyod 'bras bu smin 
59.14(1): par shog /bdag ni khams gsum 'gro drug snang yul du/ dal 'byor rgyud dul 
59.15(1): kun gyi yid du 'ong / gong dang mi 'gal gnod pa'i sems dang bral/ 'gro ba kun 
59.16(1): dang rjes su mthun par shog /bdag ni bla ma slob dpon rjes 'breng tshe/ gang 
59.17(1): gsungs dam pa'i bka' bzhin legs bsgrubs nas/ skad cig tsam yang thugs 
59.18(1): dam mi 'gal zhing / dgongs pa'i thugs bcud dag ma lon par shog /bdag ni 
59.19(1): mched lcam rnams dang 'grogs pa'i dus/ chags sdang dbang gi gnod pa'i sems 
59.20(1): bral nas/ brtse gdung gus pas sdong dang grogs gyur te/ dam tshig rnam dag skyo 
59.21(1): ngal med par shog /bdag ni g.yung drung bon la spyod pa la/ bdud dang srin po mu 
60.1(1): stegs las sogs pa'i/ bar mchod bgegs kyi bskyod pas mi tshugs shing / 'gal 
60.2(1): rkyen thams cad nye bar zhi bar shog /bdag ni bon spyod rgyun du skyongs pa la/
60.3(1): mched dang lcam dral dge ba'i sdong mdzad cing / gnas dang dus sogs rten 
60.4(1): 'brel 'dzom pa dang / mthun rkyen yo byad phun sum tshogs par shog /bdag ni 
60.5(1): drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma la/ rtag tu sangs rgyas 'du shes ma 'bral nas/ dus gsum

60.13(1): sangs rgyas dus 'dir thob par shog /bon sgo phyi nang gsang gsum gang spyod kyang /

60.17(1): pa'i longs spyod phun sum 'tshogs/ zad med gter la rgyun du spyod par shog /lus 
60.18(1): la na tsha sdug bsngal med pa dang / 'du ba rnam bzhi 'khrug pa'i skyon spangs nas/

60.21(1): pas ma bcing par/ zhen chags med pa'i rdul shugs spyod pa'i tshe/ ma chags 
61.1(1): mchod sbyin yongs su gtong par shog /bdag ni 'dul khrims sdom pa bsrung ba'i

61.3(1): zung 'brel nas/ 'dul ba'i mkhan slob dpang por byed par shog /bdag ni 
61.4(1): mnyam nyid bzod pa bsgom pa la/byams sdang gnyis kyi byung tshor spangs nas su/
61.5(1): dgra gnyen nye ring gnyis su med pa yis/ thams cad mnyam pa'i cha la 'khod par 
61.6(1): shog /bdag ni rang don nyams su len pa'i tshe/ le lo g.yeng skyong med pa'i brtson 
61.7(1): 'grus kyis/ thang lhod med par bon la rgyun spyod nas/ rtse gcig bsam pa mtha' 
61.8(1): ru phyin par shog /bdag ni mi ldog bsam gtan bsgom pa la/ skad cig tsam yang 
61.9(1): 'du 'bral med pa yi/ don la mi g.yeng ting 'dzin gzer theb nas/ 'gyur med 
61.10(1): g.yung drung bon dang ldan par shog /bdag ni phyi rgyud bon la spyod pa'i dus/ za 
61.11(1): 'dod grong chog mgo skor ma yin par/ bka' ni lung ltar tshul bzhin bgyis nas 
61.12(1): kyang / 'gro ba sems can kun la phan par shog /bdag ni 'phan yul 'don 
61.13(1): mchod spyod pa'i tshe/ dig lkugs tshig gi bar chod med pa dang / gtsang dag dam 
61.14(1): tshig gzhung ltar spyod pa yi/ khams gsum sems can thar par 'dren par shog /
61.15(1): bdag ni gsang sngags bon la spyod pa'i tshe/ bskyed rdzogs zung 'jug ya bral ma 
61.16(1): yin par/ snang sems dbyer med gcig tu rtogs pa yis/ lus ngag yid gsum 
61.17(1): lha skur bgrub par shog /bdag ni theg chen don la sgom pa'i tshe/ rtag chad gol 
61.18(1): ba'i mtha' ru ma ltung par/ bde stong gsal gsum gcig tu 'dres pa yis/ mi 
61.19(1): rtog dgongs pa rgyud la 'char bar shog /bdag ni nyams len 'du 'bral ma yin 
61.20(1): par/ rtse gcig theg pa chen po'i don rtogs nas/ rtag tu 'bral med don la rab 
61.21(1): spyod de/ bla med theg chen don dam mthar phyin shog /bdag ni spros bral chen po'i 
62.1(1): lta ba la/ bdag 'dzin 'khrul pa'i skyon rnams rab spangs nas/ sems nyid stong
